<user_name>Irasema Avila</user_name>< time>
1475089956936</time>
<Rating>1<//Rating>< Text>
I would not award them any stars.  I am very disappointed with this library.  They are not honoring their mission statement.  They are not providing free and equal access to resources or services.  I just relocated to Oxnard and I don't have access to a printer at home.  I went to the library to print out paperwork that I need to enroll my son in preschool. I took my 3 year old son in the stroller.  When I entered the computer lab I was informed that strollers were prohibited.  I was also informed that I would not be able to use the computer since their policy "printed in black and white" indicates that there is only "one person per computer" and my 3 year old son and I count as 2 people. By the way, this policy for the computer lab is not posted on their website.  It is posted by the computer lab.   I informed the attendant that my son would not be accessing the computer.  The attendant then informed me that I would have to use the computers outside the lab and that he could waive the two dollar fee.  Yes that would have been fine, but in the future when I go to the library with all of my children I will be restricted to use the computers outside of the lab and pay two dollars an hour.  This is a discriminatory practice against families.
This is incredibly disappointing.  My kids love spending time at the library.  I will not be a patron at this library or any of them in the county for that matter.  I will not allow my children to be patrons either.  I will not support an institution that has such discriminatory practices against families.

Mission statement--"The mission of the Oxnard Public Library is to enrich the lives of our diverse community by providing free and equal access to the resources, services, and programs that encourage life-long learning and lead to future success.

Offer open access to all library resources
Provide quality customer service
Lead the way to life-long learning"< /Text>

< Text>
My favorite library in the local area. Friendly staff. Selection of books, periodicals, tapes, etc. seems to have gone down recently.  Still the free wi-fi, quiet, and comfortable settings makes this a nice place to read.

The Oxnard Public Library is a free public library system operated by the City of Oxnard, California. It has three locations: the Downtown Main Library, the South Oxnard Branch Library, and the Colonia Branch Library.

The main downtown library moved from the Carnegie building to a larger facility in 1963 and again in 1992. Through the mid-to-late 20th century the library also expanded its service throughout the city of Oxnard beyond the main building, first by offering bookmobile service (1956-1989) and then by opening additional branch locations. The South Oxnard Branch opened in 1989 and moved into a new facility in 2007. Colonia Branch, a small neighborhood branch adjacent to Del Sol Park, opened in 1978.<//Text>

< review>
We had an air conditioning system replaced on an older Buick about 10 months ago using a NAPA compressor.  When the compressor failed in Austin Texas last month NAPA said they would replace the compressor but not pay for the nearly thousand dollars in labor costs.  It seemed to me and to Mike at Golden Wrench that the labor was not the issue but the compressor was but NAPA would not warranty the labor even though the installation was not the problem.  Mike at Golden Wrench really stepped up and took care of the labor even though it was not technically his problem' the problem was with NAPA. The problem took several weeks to solve but after a lot of persistence by both Mike and myself the garage in Texas replaced the failed compressor and Golden Wrench picked up the labor charge.  I really respect the way Mike and Golden Wrench stepped up and handled the problem rather than hiding behind technicalities the way NAPA did.  Golden Wrench was great but NAPA has sadly gone the way of most huge corporate entities that farm out their work to cheap Chinese companies who couldn't care less about quality.  Avoid NAPA at all costs but don't lump Golden Wrench into that category.  Excellent Garage!<//review>
